English

When it is said that “he (the sacrificer) goes on a journey for a longer time,”12 it is presumed that he should not go on a journey for a period longer than a year. If he goes on a journey for a period longer than a year, he should perform the Pavitreс╣гс╣нi. One who is going to perform this Iс╣гс╣нi procures a piece of gold. Now (the puronuv─Бky─Бs and y─Бjy─Бs) of the principal offerings: those for Pavam─Бna Agni are: “O Agni, thou purifiest life; do thou give food and strength to us. Do thou drive away ill fortune.”21 “O Agni, doing good work, do thou promote vigour and valour for us granting me prosperity and wealth.”22 For Priya Sarasvat─л: “Sarasvat─л, beloved among the beloved, having seven sisters, very agreeable, has become worthy of praise. O Sarasvat─л, these offerings are made to thee with obeisance. Do thou accept our song of praise. May we be in the most beloved favour, resorting to thee like a tree serving as a guardian.”23 For P─Бvaka Agni: “O P─Бvaka Agni, do thou bring the gods through brilliant and gentle speech, and carry their oblations. -O P─Бvaka Agni, do thou, brilliant, bring the gods here, and carry our sacrificial oblation towards them.”22 For Satyaprasava Savitr╠е: “We invoke with our implorings the universal god, lord of all that exists, Savitr╠е, who impels all that exists. God Savitr╠е comes up with his golden chariot, beholding all beings, turning up again and again along the true region and setting the mortal and immortal.”24 For ┼Ъuci Agni: “Agni with the most brilliant vow, wise, learned, shines brightly when offering is made to him. -O Agni, thy lustrous flames, shining, brilliant, are coming up.”25 For Niyutvant V─Бyu: “May the advancing V─Бyu, being gratified with offerings, gentle, come to the sacrifice with mental speed together with gentle mares.”26 O V─Бyu, I carry to thee standing among the gods in heaven the essence of sweet Soma which is bright. O God, well ascending, do thou come for drinking Soma with the chariot carried by mares. For Vratapati Agni : “O god Agni, thou art the guardian of ordinances among the mortals; thou art worthy of being honoured in sacrifice.тАФ O gods, we the ignorant have violated the ordinances promulgated by you who are wise. May Agni the wise compensate all of them with those acts with which he enables the gods to enjoy the offerings.”27 For Sipivista Viс╣гс╣Зu : “O Sipivista, I, knowing thy forms and devoted to thee, praise thy name. Being feeble, I praise thee, stronger and residing beyond this midregion. O Vi╚Щ┼Жu, what is censurable in that thou sayest “I am covered?” Do thou not conceal this (name) from us even though thou hast a different (feeble) form at the meet (with the demons at dawn).”28 For Vai┼Ыv─Бnara Agni; “May Vai┼Ыv─Бnara Agni come to us with his favour from a long distance as a result of our song capable of bringing him.-Vai┼Ыv─Бnara Agni attached to the heaven, attached to the earth, attached he has entered all plants. May he, attached severely, guard us against injury by day and at night.”29 For Dadhikr├дvan, “I have sung the praise of Dadhikr─Бvan, the swift strong horse. May he make our mouth fragranti may he prolong our life. Dadhikra, with his glory, has overspread the five peoples, as the sun with his light the waters. On the Upavasatha day of the first Iс╣гс╣нi, one should consign the sacred fires into the kindling woods, move away, churn outfire; or he should carry the permanently maintained fires. English

(The day and night) poured out paddy for cooked rice to Ahoratra of two varieties white and black, to be cooked in the milk of a white cow and a black cow both being the calves of the same mother-cow. Having allowed some time to pass, he should pour out (paddy) by day and make the offering after sunset. Or he may pour out during the (morning) twilight and offer during the (evening) twilight. He should make the offering in accordance with the time of pouring out of the oblation-material. Now the cooked rice for Uс╣гas. Having allowed the time to pass, one should pour out (paddy) at night, and make the offering at dawn. He pours out paddy for cooked rice to nakс╣гatra (in general).

English

The period of Full-moon and New-moon sacrifices and the Agnihotra does not pass away nor it becomes disturbed, so is it said. The period of evening Agnihotra does not pass away until the (next) morning Agnihotra; the period of morning Agnihotra does not pass away until the evening Agnihotra. If the evening (Agnihotra is belated), one should make an offering with the formula, “Obeisance to the illuminator of dark in the evening sv─Бh─Б,тАЭ and then offer the Agnihotra. If the morning (Agnihotra is belated), one should make an offering with the formula, “Obeisance to the illuminator of dark in the morning sv─Бh─Б,” and then offer the Agnihotra. If the ─Аhavan─лya becomes extinguished after the first Agnihotra-offering is made, one should place a piece of gold on a chip of wood with the formula, “Agni is in the wood, in the wood is Agni” and then make the second offering. If the proper time for the Agnihotra is transgressed, the practice of offering the Agnihotra in emergency should be adhered to.66

English

The time for the Full-moon sacrifice does not pass over until the time for the New-moon sacrifice; the time for the New-moon sacrifice does not pass over until the time for the Full-moon sacrifice. The time for the ┼Ъy─Бm─Бk─Бgrayaс╣Зa does not pass over until the time for Vrihy─Бgrayaс╣Зa. The time for the Vrihy─Бgrayaс╣Зa does not pass over until the time for the Yav─Бgrayana. The time for the Yav─Бgrayaс╣Зa does not pass over until the time for the Sy─Бm─Бk─Бgrayana. The time for the Vai┼Ыvadevaparvan (of the C─Бturm─Бsyas) does not pass over until the time for the Varuс╣Зapragh─Бsaparvan. The time for the Varuс╣Зapraghasaparvan does not pass over until the time for the S─Бkamedhaparvan. The time for the Sakamedhaparvan does not pass over until the time for the ┼Ъun─Бs─лr─лyaparvan. The time for the ┼Ъun─Бs─лr─лyaparvan does not pass over until the time for the Vai┼Ыvadevaparvan (in the next cycle). The time for the Animal-sacrifice pertaining to the northern course of the sun does not pass over until the time for the Animal-sacrifice pertaining to the southern course of the sun. The time for the Animal-sacrifice pertaining to the southern course of the sun does not pass over until the time for the Animal-sacrifice pertaining to the northern course of the sun. The time for the performance of the Jyotiс╣гс╣нoma to be performed in the former Vasanta does not pass over until the time for the Jyotiс╣гс╣нoma to be performed in the latter Vasanta.

for the Prastara, Barhis, separating blades, strainer, cord for the sacrificial post, sticks, strewing grass, concealment, seat, bed and introduction of a Stotra.
